# Fault Localization: iwlwifi Missing PCI Subdevice Entries

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of torvalds/linux)
- **Kernel Version**: 5.6-rc2
- **Difficulty**: expert
- **Category**: fault_localization
- **Subsystem**: Drivers
- **Component**: network-wireless (Intel iwlwifi)

## Bug Report

**Bug ID**: 206661
**Summary**: iwlwifi:9260: missing PCI subdevice entries for 0x2526 (0x04010, 0x4018 and 0x401C)
**Regression**: Yes

I am using Kernel 5.6 RC2 and I am seeing issues where firmware is not being loaded for my Intel Corporation Wireless-AC 9260 card. Attached is the boot logging.

If I can do anything to debug, let me know.

## Task

You are a fault localization agent. Given the bug report above, your task is to identify the **exact source file(s)** and **function(s)/data structure(s)** in the Linux kernel source tree (at `/workspace`) that need to be modified to fix this bug.

You must:
1. Analyze the bug report to understand the symptoms and context
2. Search the kernel source code to identify the relevant subsystem and files
3. Narrow down to the specific file(s) and function(s)/data structure(s) that contain the bug or need modification
4. Write your findings to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` in the following format:

```json
{
  "buggy_files": ["path/to/file.c"],
  "buggy_functions": ["function_or_struct_name"],
  "confidence": 0.8,
  "reasoning": "Brief explanation of why these locations are the fault"
}
```

**Important**: Paths should be relative to the kernel source root (e.g., `kernel/sched/core.c`, not `/workspace/kernel/sched/core.c`).

## Success Criteria

- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy file(s)
- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy function(s) or data structure(s)
- [ ] Write results to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json`
- [ ] Provide reasoning for the localization

- **Time limit**: 1800 seconds
- Run `bash /tests/test.sh` to verify your findings

Based on the bug report, the missing PCI subdevice IDs for device 0x2526 are:

- 0x04010
- 0x4018
- 0x401C

These entries were absent from the iwlwifi driver's PCI subdevice list, causing firmware loading failures for Intel Wireless-AC 9260 cards in kernel 5.6 RC versions.

56-assistanttext-
Now I have all the information I need. The bug is clear: the `iwl_dev_info_table` array in `drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c` is missing three entries for device 0x2526 (Intel Wireless-AC 9260) with subdevice IDs 0x0401, 0x4018, and 0x401C.

These missing entries cause the firmware to not be loaded correctly because:
1. The PCI device ID table (`iwl_hw_card_ids`) has a catch-all entry with `PCI_ANY_ID` for subdevice
2. The device info table (`iwl_dev_info_table`) is searched for more specific matches during probe
3. If specific subdevice IDs are not in the table, they fall through to the generic catch-all config instead of getting the correct 9260-specific firmware configuration

Let me create the fault localization result:

     9→  "reasoning": "The iwl_dev_info_table (device info table) in drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c is missing three IWL_DEV_INFO entries for device 0x2526 (Intel Wireless-AC 9260) with subdevice IDs 0x0401, 0x4018, and 0x401C. The table currently has entries for subdevice IDs 0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C, 0x6010, 0x6014, 0x8010, 0x8014, 0xA014, 0xE010, 0xE014 (iwl9260 variants), and 0x0030, 0x0038, 0x003C, 0x4030 (iwl9560 variants), but lacks the three mentioned subdevice entries. When a device with these subdevice IDs is enumerated, the iwl_pci_probe function searches this table for device/subdevice-specific configuration. Without matching entries, the device falls through to the catch-all PCI_ANY_ID entry which uses a generic configuration instead of the proper iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg configuration, causing firmware loading failures. The fix requires adding three new IWL_DEV_INFO macro invocations to the iwl_dev_info_table for subdevice IDs 0x0401, 0x4018, and 0x401C with the iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg configuration and iwl9260_160_name name string, similar to the existing 0x001x entries."
    10→}

61-assistanttext-
Perfect! I have successfully completed the fault localization analysis. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Fault Localization Summary

**Buggy File:** `drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c`

**Buggy Data Structure:** `iwl_dev_info_table` 

**Missing Entries:** Three IWL_DEV_INFO entries for device 0x2526 with subdevice IDs:
- 0x0401
- 0x4018  
- 0x401C

**Root Cause:** 
The device info table used by the `iwl_pci_probe()` function is missing specific entries for these three subdevice IDs. When Intel Wireless-AC 9260 cards with these PCI subdevice IDs are enumerated, the driver cannot find a matching entry in the device info table and falls back to the catch-all PCI device ID entry with `PCI_ANY_ID`. This causes the device to be configured with the generic `iwl9000_trans_cfg` configuration instead of the correct `iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg` configuration, resulting in firmware loading failures.

**Impact:** Firmware loading failures for Intel Wireless-AC 9260 cards with these specific OEM variants.

The fault localization result has been written to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` with 95% confidence.

**Sources:**
- [Linux Kernel Bug 206661 - iwlwifi:9260: missing PCI subdevice entries for 0x2526](https://bugzilla.kernel.org/show_bug.cgi?id=206661)
- [Ubuntu Bug Report on iwlwifi Intel 9260](https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/linux/+bug/1871430)

The table currently has entries for subdevice IDs 0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C, 0x6010, 0x6014, 0x8010, 0x8014, 0xA014, 0xE010, 0xE014 (iwl9260 variants), and 0x0030, 0x0038, 0x003C, 0x4030 (iwl9560 variants), but lacks the three mentioned subdevice entries. When a device with these subdevice IDs is enumerated, the iwl_pci_probe function searches this table for device/subdevice-specific configuration. Without matching entries, the device falls through to the catch-all PCI_ANY_ID entry which uses a generic configuration instead of the proper iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg configuration, causing firmware loading failures. The fix requires adding three new IWL_DEV_INFO macro invocations to the iwl_dev_info_table for subdevice IDs 0x0401, 0x4018, and 0x401C with the iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg configuration and iwl9260_160_name name string, similar to the existing 0x001x entries.\"\n}\n",

The table currently has entries for subdevice IDs 0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C, 0x6010, 0x6014, 0x8010, 0x8014, 0xA014, 0xE010, 0xE014 (iwl9260 variants), and 0x0030, 0x0038, 0x003C, 0x4030 (iwl9560 variants), but lacks the three mentioned subdevice entries.
